found = true; } }); // If no matching entry was found, create a new one if (!found) { const lastEntry = campaignTrail_temp.answer_score_state_json[campaignTrail_temp.answer_score_state_json.length - 1]; const newEntry = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(lastEntry)); // Clone the last entry newEntry.pk = lastEntry.pk + 1; newEntry.fields.affected_candidate = affectedCandidate; newEntry.fields.answer = answer; newEntry.fields.state = state; newEntry.fields.state_multiplier = changeAmount; // Overwrite state_multiplier with changeAmount campaignTrail_temp.answer_score_state_json.push(newEntry); } } //directly change support for a candidate in all (default), one or some states (takes int or array of ints as argument for state id). Careful - takes one extra turn to take effect function applyDrift(candidateId, driftAmount, stateId=undefined) { // Loop through each object in the JSON array campaignTrail_temp.candidate_state_multiplier_json.forEach((item) => { // Check if the candidate ID matches the given candidate if (item.fields.candidate === candidateId) { // If stateId is undefined or empty, apply drift to all states for that candidate if (stateId === undefined || stateId.length === 0) { item.fields.state_multiplier += driftAmount; item.fields.state_multiplier = Math.max(0, item.fields.state_multiplier); // Ensure the multiplier never goes below 0 } else { // If stateId is an array, loop through it if (Array.isArray(stateId)) { if (stateId.includes(item.fields.state)) { item.fields.state_multiplier += driftAmount; item.fields.state_multiplier = Math.max(0, item.fields.state_multiplier); // Ensure the multiplier never goes below 0 } } else { // If stateId is a single value, just check it if (item.fields.state === stateId) { item.fields.state_multiplier += driftAmount; item.fields.state_multiplier = Math.max(0, item.fields.state_multiplier); // Ensure the multiplier never goes below 0 } } } } }); } function PierceNomination() { console.log("pierce nominated"); campaignTrail_temp.candidate_json[0]["fields"].first_name = 'Franklin'; “Congratulations, Mr. Pierce, you have won the 1852 election!”

The results are soon confirmed, and it appears that Whig losses in the South combined with the Democracy's natural strength were enough to propel you to victory.

You look at your wife, and you know that she is displeased. Is that what you wanted? Soon the tremendous duty of having to select a cabinet and draft a program to be highlighted in your inaugural address falls unto your shoulders. Let's hope that everything will turn out for the best.

A Moment of Clarity

You blame yourself for your foolishness. It did not. On your inaugural trip, you saw your son's body being teared apart, leaving your wife to retire in a secluded, mystical life. Then it was William King, and after him, Charles G. Atherton, whom you had intended to make your spokesman in the Senate. A veil of mourning smothered Washington, and you returned to drinking.

Policy matters did not help you, in light of these hardships. By trying to conciliate every faction of the Democracy, from Jefferson Davis to the Barnburners, you ended up with a thousand knives pointed on your throat. Trying to salvage your ambitious plans of domination in Central America, you let Southern senators have their way with the Kansas-Nebraska Act. Civil strife ensued, you had their blood on your hands, you had Sumner's blood on your hands, and that French buffoon Pierre Soulé scuttled the acquisition of Cuba that could have saved your reputation. Hated by your own party, you lost renomination to James Buchanan, and retired from the political arena in shame.

A Moment of Clarity

You could have redeemed yourself. Instead, when the Civil War erupted, you did little to hide your sympathy for the Confederate cause, losing the last ounce of respect that your constituents once had for you. Even Hawthorne's family repudiated you, and you were not allowed to serve as his pallbearer. Now you are left to die alone.

Darling... what is it inside that bottle that makes it look so friendly?
